2006

The Finance Agenda Poll, Bids Reports (Sections I and IA) and Highway Bills dated July 24,
2006 respectively were previously approved by poll on July 28, 2006. In accordance with
Rule 4-2(c), the vote on the poll taken 7/28/06 is as follows: 8 Yeas; 1 Nay (Commissioner
Collins); 7 Divided ; and 1 Excused Absence (President Stroger).

280447, 280449, 280451 , 280457, 280459, 280462, 280475 and 280443. With respect to
the Bids Reports, Commissioner Gorman voted no on Contract Numbers 04-84-798 Rebid,

Hansen voted present on Communication Numbers 280463, 280409, 280410, 280411 ,
280412, 280413 and 280414. With respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Hansen
voted no on Contract Numbers 04-84-798 Rebid , 06-84-431 , 06-72-283 Rebid, 06-72-352,
06-82-393 and 06-54-394.

Numbers 280460 and 280434. With respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Moreno
voted present on Contract Number 06-72-359. Commissioner Peraica voted no on

respect to the Bids Reports, Commissioner Quigley voted no Contract Number 06-72-359.

INDUSTRIAL COMMISSION CLAIMS
THE FOLLOWING INDUSTRIAL COMMISSION CLAIMS SUBMITIED BY RICHARD A. DEVINE, STATE'S
ATTORNEY, RECOMMENDING PAYMENT TO THE FOLLOWING CLAIMANTS FOR INJURIES SUSTAINED IN
THE COURSE OF THEIR EMPLOYMENT, HAVE BEEN APPROVED AND RECOMMENDED FOR PAYMENT BY
THE INDUSTRIAL CLAIMS SUBCOMMITIEE:

280409

THOMAS WILCOX, in the course of his employment as a Deputy Sheriff for the
Sheriff's Court Services Division sustained accidental injuries on October 22,
2002. The accident occurred when the Petitioner caught his foot on an
elevation in the carpeting and fell to the floor, and as a result he injured his left
knee (twisting of knee, lateral subluxation of patella, moderate joint effusion).
On May 15, 2006 the Arbitrator entered a decision awarding the Petitioner the
sum of $12,341.74. State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is submitting
Industrial Commission Decision of Arbitrator, Award No. 02-WC-56781 in the
amount of $12,341 .74 and recommends its payment. (Finance Subcommittee
July 11, 2006). Attorney: Richard W. Baum, Law Firm of Baum, Ruffolo &
Marzal, Ltd .
*This item was previously approved by poll on 7/28/2006

280410

December 14, 2001 . The accident occurred when the Petitioner was struck by
a motor vehicle while crossing the street at 26th and California, and as a result
he injured his left leg and head (multiple blunt trauma, scalp lacerations with
sutures, loss of #31 tooth, loss of consciousness, torn posterior cruciate
ligament, torn medial cruciate ligament and medial meniscus, surgery to repair

meniscus). On March 4, 2004 the Arbitrator entered a decision awarding the
Petitioner the sum of $72,228.83. State's Attorney, Richard A. Devine, is
submitting Industrial Commission Decision of Arbitrator, Award No. 02-WC9561 in the amount of $72,228.83 and recommends its payment. (Finance
Subcommittee July 11, 2006). Attorney: Larry Mack, Law Firm of Steven G.
Pinto, Ltd.
